            int iCount = 0;
            while (it.hasNext()) {
                Map.Entry<String, Integer> entry = it.next();

                for(int i = 0; i < 100; i++)
                {
                    if(iCount > 0)
                        builderData.append(",");

                    builderData.append("{");

                    builderData.append(JSONObject.quote(key + String.valueOf(i)));
                    builderData.append(":");

                    iCount++;
                }
            }
            builderData.append("]");
